Collected Speeches of Reverend Sun Myung Moon
579
Compiled by the Editorial Committee for the Speeches of Reverend Sun Myung Moon

Foreword
In the beginning, God created the heavens and the earth with His Word and intended to establish Adam and Eve, the ancestors of humankind, at the center to fulfill the ideal of His Word. However, Adam and Eve distrusted the Word and fell, resulting in a world centered on Satan and sin. Consequently, God has revealed His Word according to the spiritual and intellectual development of humankind throughout different eras to restore the ideal of His Word. The fulfillment of God's promises through His Word has depended on the fulfillment of human responsibility. This central history has progressed through the Old Testament era with Moses, the New Testament era with Jesus, and has reached the final era of the Completed Testament. The Completed Testament era is the era of the fulfillment of God's long-promised ideal through the earthly manifestation of the True Parents, who are the embodiment of the completed Word.
On April 17, 1935, in his hometown of Jeongju, Pyeonganbuk-do, Reverend Moon had a spiritual encounter with Jesus during a prayer on a mountain, receiving God's official call to His providential course and beginning his public life. Over the next decade, he explored both the spiritual and physical worlds, dedicating himself to prayer, truth-seeking, and a life of empathy, through which he discovered and systematized the fundamental truth of the Principle, the Word of heavenly law.
Immediately after Korea's liberation in 1945, he began spreading the Word and engaged in providential activities for the restoration of the nation and the world. During this process, he endured six imprisonments due to misunderstanding, opposition, and persecution from established religious and political circles, walking a path of extreme suffering. However, with the transformative power of true love, which is the core value of the new Word, he naturally subdued all adversarial forces. In January 2001, he achieved a historic victory by holding the Coronation Ceremony for God's Kingship and being acclaimed as the King of Peace by leaders from various fields worldwide.
Reverend Moon came as the embodiment of God's true love, true life, and true lineage, and through the history of the Word and blessings, he bequeathed these to humanity. His path was that of a true parent, a true teacher, and a true owner. Throughout his life, he lived sacrificially, wearing the body of a servant with the heart of a parent, shedding sweat for the earth, tears for humanity, and blood for heaven. Not only did he reveal profound heavenly truths and teach them day and night, but he also thoroughly practiced them as a model, consistently living a life of giving with the heart of true love.
Reverend Moon's Word is an infinite source of life that awakens fallen humanity from ignorance and death. Since the creation of a counterpart of true love is only possible by investing more than one's life force, he devoted and committed his entire life to imparting the Word. Although the themes, dimensions, and scope of the Word vary according to the progressive stages of providence, the conditions of the era, and the audience, its consistent goal has been the completion of the providence of true love.
Reverend Moon's speeches have been officially recorded since April 1956 and have been provided in written, audio, and video formats according to the practical needs and circumstances of the time. From 1983, a comprehensive compilation effort began, culminating in the publication of 593 volumes of collected speeches on the occasion of the second year of Cheon Gi. This is an unprecedented and unparalleled masterpiece in history, both in quantity and quality, and is a legacy for all humanity to preserve for generations.
Reverend Moon's speeches are the highest scripture, exemplary sermon collections, and public lecture collections. Leaders from various fields in America and the world have praised Reverend Moon as the champion who knows best about God, Satan, humanity, the spirit world, Jesus, the Bible and scriptures, human history, and the value of true families. Such evaluations are thoroughly verified and proven throughout Reverend Moon's speeches.
The Word encompasses the essence of theories in various fields of human society, including the view of God, humanity, the universe, history, religion, politics, society, culture, and art, based on absolute values. The diversity of the Word is so deep and wide that it can be said to encompass all the large and small themes that can be experienced in the lives of humanity in this era. Its flow is like a majestic consistency or unity that originates from a deep mountain valley and winds through a great river to form an ocean. It is indeed like a grand voyage of truth.
The Word is composed with a rich blend of spirituality and intellect, religious essence and scientific information, philosophical depth, and literary and poetic descriptions. It maintains a lofty dignity and calm comfort, hot passion and tranquility, and like the alternation of day and night, sincerity and confidentiality are harmonized. The captivating power of the original emotional language leads to constant admiration. There is humor and laughter that make one burst into laughter, and stories of twists and turns that make one weep in sorrow. It transcends time, immersing one in a sense of unity that resonates and moves. It is truly the proclamation of heavenly Word and the pinnacle of human language.
Reverend Moon stated that the Word is a record of victory in life, a proclamation and declaration to humanity and future history, and the mother of heavenly law. By living according to the Word, one can enter and dwell in the liberated and released realm of the earthly kingdom beyond the realm of the fall. By becoming one with the Word, one gains the right of counterpart and resonance with the same connection. Therefore, the Word possesses an absolute nature that does not allow any artificial additions or subtractions and exercises the stern power of the iron rod throughout history.
We, the beneficiaries of this providential grace, who have received such a valuable and unchanging treasure without cost, are truly blessed and happy. Therefore, we must strive even more to create a world of peace and ideal completion of the Word through a life of constantly reading, practicing, and spreading the Word. In doing so, we must offer infinite gratitude, praise, and glory to God and the True Parents, who are the ultimate owners of the Word, with the substantial results of our fruits. *

Editorial Office

················································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································ That's why Barrytown graduates, seminary graduates, if you studied hard, you should have graduated thousands, hundreds of people.... Why don't you evangelize? If you worked as hard as I did, it would be difficult to even accept those students, graduates.

The Korean people are an excellent people
In modern cultural history, you cannot remove the name of Reverend Moon. That's the problem. Even if you don't like it, saying things you don't like is to save you. It's to teach and correct you. I have never thought of America collapsing. What is it? Even in Danbury, there are all sorts of people. They tried to ruin the line they were living on, ruin the entire vicinity, and did all sorts of schemes, but I have never thought like that.

In prison, in Danbury, if it's Danbury, I created a group of people who would say they would follow me when I came out. I didn't come out with debts, I made them owe debts. That's right.

Why do they talk about Hawaii? The mountains are well-formed. There are four islands, but there are eight. What is the four-position foundation? Isn't the four-position foundation a couple of eight? Big ones, small ones, eight. When it's the big one, the father, there are four people. When it's the son, there are four people, so it's the number 8. Four times eight is thirty-two (4×8=32). Four times eight is thirty-two (4×8=32), thirty-two! Teeth are thirty-two.

So, the age of 16 is the problem. The teacher also received the first prize at the World Poets Association. It was a prayer title written at the age of sixteen. It was announced after 72 years. Eight times nine is seventy-two (8×9=72). So, numbers and heavenly principles must match. Can you just attach them and make them match? You need to know that.

Why did Yang Chang-shik go in? Who told him to go in? (Laughter) This guy also does what he wants like an American. The teacher didn't tell him to sit, I didn't tell him to go in, but he went in and is doing something. The words aren't even finished.... This person will also be taken. (Laughter)

If you take away Koreans from America, it will be difficult if 2 million are taken away. "Will God take away the Jewish people from America, or will He take away only Koreans?" God will not take away the Jewish people. He will take away the Korean people. It's special. If there are Koreans in your neighborhood, just watch.

In the current global scientific standard, companies like the Korean company are ranked 1st, 2nd, 3rd, 4th, 5th globally. Do you know that? And they have already made and are using in practice submarines that can attack and defend simultaneously by launching satellites and breaking through ice over 2 meters. Do you know that?

America is worried that they might sell it. They have made ships that can break and crush ice while running at normal speed and are selling them to Russia. Do you know that?

In Korea, there is a war museum. Is there a war museum in America? There are memorials, but no museums. In Korea, there is a war museum. Because they research the shortcomings and everything else, what will happen in 10 years?
How does it feel when a teacher departs from this world? The Korean people are an outstanding nation in front of the world. The Dongyi people ruled over China, Mongolia, the Mongolian world, and the entire Asian region. They were skilled in war and archery, and their mental unity was swift. Wherever they went, they were victorious in every battle. 

After winning a hundred times, what happens is... Even though there was only one enemy, after winning, two or three would unite. That's why they disliked war and preferred peace, avoiding war on the Korean Peninsula. There's no one else like them! They didn't spread out to the continent in all directions but blocked the Yalu River here, built a fence, and lived well. However, their nature is destined by heaven to live for the world. If they don't live for the world, they will be trampled before the world. 

Therefore, they must win in front of them. They must win against the Soviet Union, China, Japan, and the United States. They have trained for this. Americans cannot digest Korea. Neither can the Japanese, Chinese, nor Russians. They all come and go. They come to consume but end up vomiting it out. When they vomit, they must even vomit out their own belly button. 

Think lightly of Korea. Koreans are the most fearsome people. I know. Among them, I am the most fearsome. I know. On the day I decide, the world will be in trouble. "Amen!" (Applause) 

Until you conclude your path, you must go cleanly without deviating. Communism went on a path of purging. What happens if you purge your enemies? If you have such a mindset, you wouldn't leave a single person. That's why when I go hunting in the mountains or catch fish in the sea, even if I shoot the first one I intended to catch, I don't kill it. If it becomes disabled, I let it go. The personality is frightening. It's someone who sees things through to the end. 

Can the CIA in America defeat Reverend Moon? Can the UN defeat Reverend Moon? Can the USA defeat Reverend Moon? The North Korean issue, the Soviet issue, the Chinese issue, and the European issue are all blocked. 

Reverend Moon has not emphasized America but the maritime realm, as mentioned in Chapter XIII. You must know that. Until you conclude your path, don't go off course or deviate. Go cleanly, cleanly. 

Reverend Moon has been saying the same things for 50, 60 years. What he said back then is all coming true now. If you don't know, ask. Yang Chang-shik, do you know that? "Yes." Is everything the teacher says correct? "Yes, it is." 

It's the same now. Let them all boast about how great they are. Those who graduated from Seoul National University and studied abroad to get their doctorates have all been shattered. Those who left the Unification Church, saying it was heretical and teaching against it in theological schools, are now at a point where their tongues can be pulled out. You must wake up, everyone. 

How fearsome is the Soviet Union? How fearsome is the CIA in America? The KGB and the CIA fight well, don't they? It's not to help anyone. It's to survive. Reverend Moon says he will save both while sacrificing. Isn't that right? The KGB, the CIA... 

When I brought 4,000 people from the Soviet Union to educate them, the KGB stamped it blindly. The CIA thought Reverend Moon would ruin everything, but they realized he was trying to save the communists for America's sake. The communists think so too. They say the KGB is being saved. There are such facts... If you wait and see, you'll know what's right and wrong. If you save those who are about to die and let those who are alive live well... There's no democratic world that can treat you well. 

You must maintain balance. 

First themselves, first relatives...! Can brothers eat together? You don't know how big this universe is. Do the stars eat together as brothers? When big and small things unite and lack strength, they always die. You must maintain balance. Balance is needed. Everything lives by maintaining balance. 

Where there is no balance, where balance cannot be maintained, there can be no horizon. The horizon comes first. Horizon, horizon! Things must be similar; if both are great, they fight. If there's the greatest and the least, the greatest person doesn't seek out the greatest person. They must seek out the least person. That way, the future is long. You must find a protector. 

Standing at the forefront of America, the least country is treated like a mutt, and the greatest country... Is there a country greater than America? They believe in God but don't know God? If they don't know God, it ends there! Can a great person come and win against a thousand or ten thousand people in arm wrestling? On the day they lose, it's all over. 

Therefore, a great person must raise the least people. If a great person has an enemy, and they fight, both disappear, but if they raise ten times or a hundred people, how can they win against a hundred people? That's what Reverend Moon says. All five races, whether at the UN or anywhere, have Reverend Moon's foundation. Isn't that right? Enemies and enemies sit here together, and Japan... *Japanese members, raise your hands. (*Spoken in Japanese) 

Is this a Japanese church or an American church? There are more than the white people. You must know that. Who will become the owner of the Pacific, the world...! Instead of America, China or the Soviet Union now in the Pacific region, the Pacific Rim region, who will they make the owner? To defeat America, they put forward the Japanese. To defeat the Japanese, they put forward the Koreans. 

Koreans have suffered the most and died the least! The Japanese have died the most. When evaluating people, how are Japanese and Americans? People with Eastern thought are better than those with Western thought, individualism. Better people have died more. 

When I came here, there were 130,000 Koreans. Now, 2.6 million have settled. Why did they come here? They came to study. They say it's good for divorce... Koreans hold the world record for divorce. Following the Americans who like divorce, they say, "Let's try it too." When they try, their sons and daughters disappear. They become hippies and yippies, and because the world history is overturned, it has become difficult. 

That's why they come to the Unification Church and hold on. I am needed for those who have divorced, centered on the Unification Church. 

Absolute Sexual Organ 

Now, Chapter IX and Chapter X, what are they? Absolute! What is absolute, Yang Chang-shik? "Yes." What is absolute? "Before marriage, absolute purity, and after marriage..." Hey, hey, I asked in English. What is absolute? "It's called absolute sex." What? Is it a sex organ, or is it a sexual organ? Absolute? "It's absolute sex." Is it sex, or is it a sexual organ? "It's keeping the sexual organ absolutely." The noun is a sex organ. Sexual is the range of action. 

Do you have an absolute sexual organ? You have a sexual organ, but you don't have an absolute sexual organ. It's strange. What does that absolute sexual organ do? You can't do it with just sexual. Absolute sexual! The absolute sexual organ, anyone can have it. You do sex, but the sexual organ becomes one because of absolute. It's representative. 

There's depth, width, and harmony there... If it's called a sexual organ, what harmony is there in sexual? "There isn't." Then why do you call it a sexual organ? It's sexual. It's absolute! "Since it's absolute, if you say absolute sexual organ, now if you say absolute sexual organ..." Since there's an organ, the action is sex. "Yes." The absolute sexual organ is the only one. 

You guys, even though you can do free sex, that's also a sexual organ... Is that also an absolute sexual? There's only one organ. You must know that. Then, when people become one, in matching the relative standard, can you say men and women are equal, that men and women cannot be separated? It's the sexual organ. 

That organ is not just for men, not just for women. There are three owners. It belongs to God, to men, and to women, but can you think of it as your own? If there's a sexual organ, do women need men's sexual organs, or not? They seek it. Men seek women's. 

You can't just leave it. It can't become a battlefield. It's good, it's the blessing of blessings, and it's the best thing that can't be exchanged for anything in the world. Have you ever thought of it as the best? Shouldn't you become one centered on the best thing? You can't buy it with money. You can't exchange it for anything. There's no concept of an absolute sexual organ, is there? Free sex, oh... It's dirty. It's dirty. 

At the ages of 25, 24, 23, I fought because of that. To protect my body, how complicated it was... When people meet me and hear my words, they go crazy with joy. They all try to take me away. They try to bury me in their tribe. I don't follow them. With money, power, knowledge...? It doesn't work. 

So, you must become the owner of the absolute sexual organ. Owner of the absolute sexual organ! That's how you know what's precious. When I went to Japan to study, I overcame countless temptations because of that. Not because of money. Even now, it's the same. In America, American women are like that, in Germany, German women are like that. 

The spirit world teaches them. "You must serve the teacher instead of your husband. Sell all your husband's property and offer it to the teacher." That's the right path. That's the right path. The stolen goods from the Garden of Eden never have an owner. When the owner appears, you must return it. If you get sick and have to cut off a hand, will you die? If you get sick, it ruins the blood vessels, and everything is cut off. It's severance, severance! Now, do you understand? "Yes." 

Cain must repent and cross over to the Abel world 

When you speak, you speak as you please. When I see it, there's no system. There must be a system. Reverend Moon spoke for 10 hours... I stood in one place and spoke for 16 hours and 47 minutes. I stayed up all night and did it all in one place. So, women who wanted to pee, men and women who wanted to poop... I saw all sorts of things below and lived. 

When the teacher speaks, it's interesting. It's tasty. Whether it's barley rice or whatever, the teacher is tasty. So they try to follow. They follow, forgetting to eat lunch, breakfast, lunch, and dinner, fearing they'll miss the teacher. Fasting is common. Even without eating for a week, they go to the labor field and work. They're peculiar people! 

Oh, let's see your face! Woman, come out. Come out and sing a song, sing! (Applause) Oh, if the teacher doesn't want to hear it, stop quickly and sing. You must cut it off! Such a woman has the talent to sing any popular song or famous song. I say it because I see it in her mouth. Sing a song! (A member sings) 

(Singing too cautiously and gently) Sing as you want, with sound! The sound is good, but don't think about doing well. Sing as if you're playing and singing. (Applause) "I'm sorry. I don't know what you said." "He said to sing naturally. (Yang Chang-shik)" "Can I sing with my husband?" Is that your wife? (Laughter) "Yes, it's his wife. (Yang Chang-shik)" "Yes, he's my husband." Well, it seems to fit well. Come out and try! (Laughter) (The couple sings together) (Applause) 

When singing like that, it's uplifting, but when you speak, the words might fly away, so what should you do? Organize the environment. "Yes, give a big hand to the couple who sang." (Applause) "This couple, despite living difficult lives, is so diligent in their missionary work. They are truly exemplary members. (Yang Chang-shik)" 

(Yang Chang-shik's report continues; ...On the 9th, a few representatives from our group, centered on Hyun Jin Nim, have been invited to Houston, Texas, where George Bush's special memorial is, to meet him and discuss the direction America should take in the future. 

With such a great providential direction, Father is tirelessly leading, reading, educating, and practicing on the front lines more diligently than us. All our young members must step forward, relieve the concerns of the Parents, and devote all efforts to establishing America before Heaven. Once again, with a warm heart, let's welcome the coming Parents and resolve to fulfill our responsibilities with a warm round of applause.) (Applause) 

Hoon Dok Hae...! "How many chapters should we do? (Yang Chang-shik)" Chapter IX and Chapter X, what are these? The number 9 is a single number, but the number 10 is a relative number. Where did it go? Wonju! "Wonju sister, come here." Where, read it well. A new start! Understand Chapter IX well. Listen carefully. Chapters VII, VIII, IX, these three chapters are indemnity. Cain must repent and cross over to the Abel world. Now...! (Peace Message Chapter IX 'God's Ideal Family and the Kingdom of Peaceful Ideal World' Hoon Dok reading is interrupted) *
